Write your plan for your next actions on the line below your action, starting with "Next actions:".\\ \tt For example:\\ \tt > open cupboard\\ \tt Next actions: take orange, eat orange\\ \tt \\ \tt Your goal for this game is: Put the book on the shelf, the sandwich on the table and the broom on the counter.\\ \tt \\ \tt Once you have achieved your goal, write "> done" to end the game.\\ \tt \\ \tt You are in a living room now. There are a side table, a couch, a chair and a shelf. There are passages to a hallway, a kitchen and a bedroom here. 
	  } 
	   }
